\begin{align*} R(\boldsymbol{u}, \boldsymbol{v}) \boldsymbol{w} &amp;= [\nabla_{\boldsymbol{u}}, \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}}] \boldsymbol{w} - \nabla_{[\boldsymbol{u}, \boldsymbol{v}]} \boldsymbol{w} \\ &amp;= \nabla_{\boldsymbol{u}} \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}} \boldsymbol{w} - \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}} \nabla_{\boldsymbol{u}} \boldsymbol{w} - \nabla_{[\boldsymbol{u}, \boldsymbol{v}]} \boldsymbol{w} \\
